<p><br/></p>
<p>The following is a list of <b>notable deaths in April 2016</b>.</p>
<p>Entries for each day are listed <u>alphabetically</u> by surname. A typical entry lists information in the following sequence:</p>
<ul>
<li>Name, age, country of citizenship and reason for notability, established cause of death, reference.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="April_2016">April 2016</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_April_2016&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: April 2016">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1">1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_April_2016&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Karl-Robert_Ameln" title="Karl-Robert Ameln">Karl-Robert Ameln</a>, 96, Swedish sailor (<a href="/wiki/1948_Summer_Olympics" title="1948 Summer Olympics">1948</a> and <a href="/wiki/1952_Summer_Olympics" title="1952 Summer Olympics">1952 Olympics</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Aleksander_Arkuszy%C5%84ski" title="Aleksander Arkuszyński">Aleksander Arkuszyński</a>, 98, Polish brigadier general, WWII veteran.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pratyusha_Banerjee" title="Pratyusha Banerjee">Pratyusha Banerjee</a>, 24, Indian actress, suicide by hanging.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alan_Carter_(civil_servant)" title="Alan Carter (civil servant)">Alan Carter</a>, 86, British civil servant, <a href="/wiki/Director_of_Immigration" title="Director of Immigration">Director of Immigration</a> of Hong Kong (1983–1989).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tom_Coughlin_(Walmart_executive)" title="Tom Coughlin (Walmart executive)">Tom Coughlin</a>, 67, American business executive and convicted fraudster (<a href="/wiki/Walmart" title="Walmart">Walmart</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/George_Curry_(American_football)" title="George Curry (American football)">George Curry</a>, 71, American football coach.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mame_Younousse_Dieng" title="Mame Younousse Dieng">Mame Younousse Dieng</a>, 76, Senegalese writer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Artur_G%C3%B3rski" title="Artur Górski">Artur Górski</a>, 46, Polish politician, member of <a href="/wiki/Sejm" title="Sejm">Sejm</a> (since 2005), leukemia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kao_Ching-yuen" title="Kao Ching-yuen">Kao Ching-yuen</a>, 87, Taiwanese businessman (<a href="/wiki/Uni-President_Enterprises_Corporation" title="Uni-President Enterprises Corporation">Uni-President Enterprises Corporation</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup> (death announced on this date)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Richard_S._Kem" title="Richard S. Kem">Richard S. Kem</a>, 89, American army Major-General.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Emil_Keres" title="Emil Keres">Emil Keres</a>, 90, Hungarian actor and theatre director.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Clarence_Makwetu" title="Clarence Makwetu">Clarence Makwetu</a>, 88, South African politician.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Herbert_Theodore_Milburn" title="Herbert Theodore Milburn">Herbert Theodore Milburn</a>, 84, American judge.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/John_Minney" title="John Minney">John Minney</a>, 76, English cricketer (<a href="/wiki/Cambridge_University_Cricket_Club" title="Cambridge University Cricket Club">Cambridge University</a>, <a href="/wiki/Northamptonshire_County_Cricket_Club" title="Northamptonshire County Cricket Club">Northamptonshire</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wiebe_Nijenhuis" title="Wiebe Nijenhuis">Wiebe Nijenhuis</a>, 61, Dutch sportsman.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Carl_Nordling" title="Carl Nordling">Carl Nordling</a>, 85, Swedish physicist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Marjorie_Peters" title="Marjorie Peters">Marjorie Peters</a>, 97, American baseball player (<a href="/wiki/All-American_Girls_Professional_Baseball_League" title="All-American Girls Professional Baseball League">AAGBPL</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Patricia_Thompson_(writer)" title="Patricia Thompson (writer)">Patricia Thompson</a>, 89, American philosopher.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9_Villers" title="André Villers">André Villers</a>, 85, French photographer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tony_Whittaker" title="Tony Whittaker">Tony Whittaker</a>, 83, British solicitor and politician.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ron_Wicks" title="Ron Wicks">Ron Wicks</a>, 76, Canadian <a href="/wiki/National_Hockey_League" title="National Hockey League">NHL</a> ice hockey referee, liver cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2">2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_April_2016&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gato_Barbieri" title="Gato Barbieri">Gato Barbieri</a>, 83, Argentine jazz saxophonist, pneumonia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rick_Bartow" title="Rick Bartow">Rick Bartow</a>, 69, American artist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Moreese_Bickham" title="Moreese Bickham">Moreese Bickham</a>, 98, American convicted murderer and anti-death penalty activist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ferrari" title="Sergio Ferrari">Sergio Ferrari</a>, 72, Italian footballer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gallieno_Ferri" title="Gallieno Ferri">Gallieno Ferri</a>, 87, Italian comic book artist (<i><a href="/wiki/Zagor" title="Zagor">Zagor</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Mister_No" title="Mister No">Mister No</a></i>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Boris_Hybner" title="Boris Hybner">Boris Hybner</a>, 74, Czech actor and mime artist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gareth_Jones_(lawyer)" title="Gareth Jones (lawyer)">Gareth Jones</a>, 85, British legal academic.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Martin_Lampkin" title="Martin Lampkin">Martin Lampkin</a>, 65, English <a href="/wiki/Motorcycle_trials" title="Motorcycle trials">motorcycle trials</a> rider, cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nabil_Nosair" title="Nabil Nosair">Nabil Nosair</a>, 77, Egyptian footballer (<a href="/wiki/Zamalek_SC" title="Zamalek SC">Zamalek</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amber_Rayne" title="Amber Rayne">Amber Rayne</a>, 31, American pornographic actress.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dennis_Riggin" title="Dennis Riggin">Dennis Riggin</a>, 79, Canadian ice hockey player (<a href="/wiki/Detroit_Red_Wings" title="Detroit Red Wings">Detroit Red Wings</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/L%C3%A1szl%C3%B3_S%C3%A1rosi_(footballer)" title="László Sárosi (footballer)">László Sárosi</a>, 84, Hungarian football player and coach.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Thomas_Zeng_Jing-mu" title="Thomas Zeng Jing-mu">Thomas Zeng Jing-mu</a>, 95, Chinese clandestine Roman Catholic prelate, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Yujiang" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Yujiang">Yujiang</a> (1988–2012).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup></li>
<li>Soldiers killed in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2016_Armenian%E2%80%93Azerbaijani_clashes" title="2016 Armenian–Azerbaijani clashes">Armenian–Azerbaijani clashes</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Robert_Abajyan" title="Robert Abajyan">Robert Abajyan</a>, 19, Armenian (<a href="/wiki/Nagorno-Karabakh_Defense_Army" title="Nagorno-Karabakh Defense Army">Nagorno-Karabakh Defense Army</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Samid_Imanov" title="Samid Imanov">Samid Imanov</a>, 34–35, Azerbaijani (<a href="/wiki/Special_Forces_of_Azerbaijan" title="Special Forces of Azerbaijan">Special Forces</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Murad_Mirzayev" title="Murad Mirzayev">Murad Mirzayev</a>, 40, Azerbaijani (<a href="/wiki/Special_Forces_of_Azerbaijan" title="Special Forces of Azerbaijan">Special Forces</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kyaram_Sloyan" title="Kyaram Sloyan">Kyaram Sloyan</a>, 19, Armenian (<a href="/wiki/Nagorno-Karabakh_Defense_Army" title="Nagorno-Karabakh Defense Army">Nagorno-Karabakh Defense Army</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="3">3</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_April_2016&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 3">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Abu_Firas_al-Suri" title="Abu Firas al-Suri">Abu Firas al-Suri</a>, 65, Syrian <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al-Nusra_Front" title="Al-Nusra Front">al-Nusra Front</a> senior official, air strike.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Phanor_Arizabaleta-Arzayus" title="Phanor Arizabaleta-Arzayus">Phanor Arizabaleta-Arzayus</a>, 78, Colombian criminal, heart attack.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/John_C._Baldwin" title="John C. Baldwin">John C. Baldwin</a>, 67, American cardiac surgeon<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/John_Vane,_11th_Baron_Barnard" title="John Vane, 11th Baron Barnard">John Vane, 11th Baron Barnard</a>, 92, British peer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Erik_Bauersfeld" title="Erik Bauersfeld">Erik Bauersfeld</a>, 93, American radio dramatist (<a href="/wiki/KPFA" title="KPFA">KPFA</a>) and voice actor (<i><a href="/wiki/Star_Wars" title="Star Wars">Star Wars</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/A.I._Artificial_Intelligence" title="A.I. Artificial Intelligence">A.I. Artificial Intelligence</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Crimson_Peak" title="Crimson Peak">Crimson Peak</a></i>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ward_Crutchfield" title="Ward Crutchfield">Ward Crutchfield</a>, 87, American politician, member of the <a href="/wiki/Tennessee_Senate" title="Tennessee Senate">Tennessee Senate</a> (1985–2007).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup></li>

Denholm</a>, 92, American politician, member of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">United States House of Representatives</a> from <a href="/wiki/South_Dakota%27s_1st_congressional_district" title="South Dakota's 1st congressional district">South Dakota's 1st congressional district</a> (1971–1975).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117"><a href="#cite_note-117">[117]</a></sup></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Hendrikje_Fitz" title="Hendrikje Fitz">Hendrikje Fitz</a>, 54, German actress (<i><a href="/wiki/In_aller_Freundschaft" title="In aller Freundschaft">In aller Freundschaft</a></i>), cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-119"><a href="#cite_note-119">[119]</a></sup>⋅</li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Cyril_Edel_Leonoff" title="Cyril Edel Leonoff">Cyril Edel Leonoff</a>, 91, Canadian civil engineer and historian.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-123"><a href="#cite_note-123">[123]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Carlo_Monti" title="Carlo Monti">Carlo Monti</a>, 96, Italian athlete, Olympic bronze medalist (<a href="/wiki/Athletics_at_the_1948_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_4_%C3%97_100_metres_relay" title="Athletics at the 1948 Summer Olympics – Men's 4 × 100 metres relay">1948</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124"><a href="#cite_note-124">[124]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Blackjack_Mulligan" title="Blackjack Mulligan">Blackjack Mulligan</a>, 73, American professional wrestler (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/World_Wrestling_Entertainment" title="World Wrestling Entertainment">WWWF</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jim_Crockett_Promotions" title="Jim Crockett Promotions">JCP</a>, <a href="/wiki/Championship_Wrestling_from_Florida" title="Championship Wrestling from Florida">CWF</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-125"><a href="#cite_note-125">[125]</a></sup></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Jimmie_Van_Zant" title="Jimmie Van Zant">Jimmie Van Zant</a>, 59, American singer, songwriter and guitarist, liver cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127"><a href="#cite_note-127">[127]</a></sup></li>
